[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer-based fuzzing run detected a critical security issue: a file path          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal vulnerability in the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” example code. The [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         fuzzer supplied crafted input that caused `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` to unpack archive  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries with path components that escape the intended output directory, triggering  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception from the FilePathTraversal sanitizer.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Issue Overview                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           A file path traversal vulnerability was identified during fuzz testing. The       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         security sanitizer raised an exception when an archive entry’s output path resolved [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to a location outside the designated extraction directory                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m…[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`[1m)[0m.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The issue is classified as “File path traversal.” This occurs when file names or  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive entry paths include sequences [1m([0me.g., “..”[1m)[0m that allow writing files to      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         locations outside the expected output directory.                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Key Observations                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. The exception originates in the Jazzer sanitizer:                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - `com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check`            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - `FilePathTraversal.checkPath` and `pathFirstArgHook` validate the first path [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         argument of file operations.                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. The sanitizer is invoked from the Expander code path:                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              -                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1m([0mExpander.jav[1;92ma:86[0m[1m)[0m`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              - Subsequent overloaded `expand` methods at lines [1;36m204[0m, [1;36m324[0m, [1;36m400[0m, and [1;36m460[0m.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. The fuzzer harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` at line [1;36m52[0m[1m)[0m serves as  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the entry point but is not the root cause.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Relevant Code Areas for Investigation                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. FilePathTraversal sanitizer logic [1m([0mFilePathTraversal.java[1m)[0m – the checks        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         applied to paths before writing files.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. Expander.expand methods in                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` – how archive entry paths [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         are processed, normalized, and combined with the output directory.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Fuzzer harness `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` – to understand input       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         handling, although it is not the vulnerability’s origin.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Investigating these areas will provide a complete view of the path traversal        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         behavior and the security checks that triggered the exception.                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:75[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m83[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:    default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:        final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:        final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        return outputFile;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:67[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m74[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    private <T extends ArchiveEntry> void [0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal ArchiveEntrySupplier<T> [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupplier, final ArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T> writer, final Path targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:            throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:        final boolean nullTarget = targetDirectory == null;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:        final Path targetDirPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:        T nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:        while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:            final Path targetPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:83[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m88[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Problem Analysis and Root Cause  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability arises in `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. It [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```java[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     but only treats the string `name` literally. On Unix, backslashes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive entry names are not recognized as separators, so sequences like [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"..\\etc\\passwd"[0m[39m` get resolved under the intended parent directory and pass the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck. Later, when the code writes out the file, the Jazzer sanitizer canonicalizes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe path and correctly detects that the output file lies outside `parentPath`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggering a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In short: mixed or non-native separators in entry names evade the existing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“zip‐slip” check.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Fix Strategy  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We will harden `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` so that it treats both forward [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mslashes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and backslashes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as path separators—regardless of the host [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOS—*before* any normalization or `startsWith` check. This ensures that traversal [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in either form are properly collapsed out and caught by the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting safety check.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Plan  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodify the default `resolveIn` implementation as follows:  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      i. Retrieve the raw entry name.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ii. Split it on both `[0m[35m/[0m[39m` and `\` into segments.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    iii. Reconstruct a `Path` by iteratively resolving those segments against the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parentPath`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     iv. Call `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the result.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      v. Retain the existing `startsWith` check to reject any path that escapes the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended directory.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This change requires no modifications to `Expander.java` or any fuzzing [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness code—thus preserving all existing functionality and test harnesses.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Example Revised Implementation  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m([0m[39minside `ArchiveEntry.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   import java.io.IOException;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   import java.nio.file.Path;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   import java.util.Objects;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mObjects.requireNonNull[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath, [0m[32m"parentPath must not be null"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Split on both Unix and Windows separators:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       String[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m segments = [0m[1;35mname.split[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32m[[0m[32m/\\\\[0m[32m][0m[32m+"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Iteratively resolve each segment under parentPath:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       Path candidate = parentPath;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString seg : segments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Preserve empty segments only if they’re significant:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mseg.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m"."[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseg[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m skip[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               candidate = [0m[1;35mcandidate.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Normalize to collapse [0m[32m"."[0m[39m and [0m[32m".."[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       candidate = [0m[1;35mcandidate.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Reject if it escapes the parent[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mcandidate.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip detected: '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                             parentPath, name, candidate[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return candidate;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We strip out both kinds of separators so that any “..” segments—regardless of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir original slash style—are normalized and can trigger the safety check.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Absolute names [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[35m/etc/[0m[95mpasswd[0m[39m` or `C:\Windows\system32`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will also be [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaught, because `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on an absolute first segment resets the path to that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegment, and the subsequent `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` fails.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch leaves intact the existing exception message format, `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand the `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` guard.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to `Expander` or fuzzer harness code, so all archive [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypes, fuzzer workflows, and example uses remain valid.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Archive entries with only native separators [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `foo/bar` on Unix or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`foo\bar` on Windows[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to work exactly as before.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Addressing the Evaluation Report  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This strategy eliminates the scenario where non-native separators evade the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal check, thus preventing the Jazzer sanitizer from ever seeing an [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munintended write outside `parentPath`.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All critical logic from the existing codebase is preserved; the sanitizing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary is left untouched.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Splitting on both separators could treat a legitimate entry name containing a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mliteral backslash [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., as metadata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as a path delimiter. However, archives in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwild rarely use mixed separators in *file* names if they intend literal [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbackslashes; and if they do, those names would be interpreted as nested [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectories, which is the safer default.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If a downstream consumer truly needs a literal backslash in the extracted file[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname, they can later rename the file, but they cannot overwrite arbitrary [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectories.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We consider this trade-off acceptable for a security-critical example.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. No Additional File Retrieval Needed  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All necessary context resides in `ArchiveEntry.java`. No further code sampling[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis required.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m            - The sanitizer hook points to the first argument of a file‐creating API [1m([0me.g.,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Files.newOutputStream`[1m)[0m, indicating the path passed was outside the parent.        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer`[1m)[0m merely feeds inputs into `Expander`; it is not  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         the root cause but exposes the traversal.                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - File modified:                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Added `import java.util.Objects;`                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In the default `[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath parentPath[1m)[0m` method:                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • `[1;35mObjects.requireNonNull[0m[1m([0mparentPath, [32m"parentPath must not be null"[0m[1m)[0m;`         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Retrieve the entry name via `[1;35mgetName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Split the name on both forward and back slashes: `String[1m[[0m[1m][0m segments =        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mname.split[0m[1m([0m[32m"[0m[32m[[0m[32m/\\\\[0m[32m][0m[32m+"[0m[1m)[0m;`                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Iteratively resolve each non‐empty, non‐“.” segment under `parentPath`.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Normalize the resulting `Path`.                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              • Verify `[1;35mcandidate.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m`, else throw `[1;35mIOException[0m[1m([0m[32m"Zip slip[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdetected: ..."[0m[1m)[0m`.                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This replaces the simpler `[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mname[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` and prefix    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         check.                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Post‐Patch Result                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:import org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.ArchiveEntry;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:import org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.EntryStreamOffsets;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:import org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.zip.ZipEncoding;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:75[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m83[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:    default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:        final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:        final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        return outputFile;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All archive‐entry paths in the Expander example funnel through the default [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` implementation.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The last patch split on separators and resolved segments one by one—but that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic still permitted some crafted names [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. names with embedded “..” that [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalize under the prefix[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or relied on per‐segment resolution rather than [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutright rejecting illegal roots.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A more serious issue is that the Expander example contains other code paths [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g. the Zip-stream and Tar-stream overloads[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that perform writes via `new [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirectory, entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` directly, bypassing our [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatched method altogether. The fuzzer’s crash still occurs at [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m86[0m[39m`, indicating resolveIn either wasn’t invoked on that [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbranch or returned a Path outside the intended root.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Strategy  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Centralize and harden path‐sanitization in `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Strip any leading separators from the raw entry name [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto neutralize [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mabsolute paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Convert the cleaned name into a relative `Path` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcleanedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Reject *any* normalized relative path that begins with `..` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindicating an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape attempt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Resolve the safe relative path against `parentPath` and return the result.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Audit **all** file‐write and directory‐create sites in `Expander.java` to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure they exclusively use `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Replace any direct `new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdir, entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparent.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls with `[0m[1;35mentry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Before writing a file or creating a directory, always call `resolveIn`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthen `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` as needed, then [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3.1[0m[39m. Revise `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Remove the per‐segment loop.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Add logic:  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           ```java[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mObjects.requireNonNull[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath, [0m[32m"parentPath must not be null"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Strip leading separators to avoid absolute paths[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               String cleaned = [0m[1;35mname.replaceFirst[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"^[0m[32m[[0m[32m/\\\\[0m[32m][0m[32m+"[0m[39m, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Build a normalized relative Path[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               Path rel = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcleaned[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Reject traversal attempts[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mrel.isAbsolute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mrel.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m".."[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                   throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                       [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip detected: [0m[32mparent[0m[32m=%s, [0m[32mentry[0m[32m=%s, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mnormalized[0m[32m=%s"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                     parentPath, name, rel[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Safe resolution under the parent[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           ```[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • This handles both Unix [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and Windows [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m separators, prohibits any [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`..` at the front of the normalized path, and cleanly resolves legitimate relative [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3.2[0m[39m. Audit `Expander.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mall overloads of `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Search for any code that does:  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          File outFile = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m or[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path outPath = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Replace each occurrence with:  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path outPath = [0m[1;35mentry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35moutPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - For directory entries, do:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path dirPath = [0m[1;35mentry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - For file entries, after the `createDirectories`, open the stream with:  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream os = [0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39moutPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Remove any remaining `File.renameTo` or `FileOutputStream` usages in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfavor of the above pattern.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By consolidating all path‐sanitization in one concise, normalization‐based [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm, we eliminate edge‐case bugs introduced by bespoke segment‐loop logic.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stripping leading separators negates absolute paths; rejecting any normalized [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath starting with `..` blocks slip attempts like `foo/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mbar[0m[39m`.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Enforcing `resolveIn` for every write/directory operation guarantees no bypass[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the security check.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach preserves existing functionality: legitimate multi‐level [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectories [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`a/b/c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, “.[0m[35m/[0m[39m” segments, and Windows‐style separators are all accepted[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand mapped under the specified `parentPath`.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side-Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entries whose names resolve to the empty string [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. an entry named `[0m[35m/[0m[39m` or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`.[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will normalize to `[0m[32m""[0m[39m` and be treated as “.`” → writes to `parentPath`. That [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis acceptable [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrepresents the archive root[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or can be further special-cased if [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundesirable.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entries that include drive‐letter syntax [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`C:\foo`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m become cleaned to `[0m[32m"C:"[0m[39m` +[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"foo"[0m[39m` segments. If that is unacceptable, add a further check on [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mrel.getNameCount[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or character set.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing unit tests and example flows that rely on `Expander` writing [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles under the target directory will continue to function, since the mapping under[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parentPath` is unchanged for legal names.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar normalization logic is used in [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Extractor`, see its use of [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m".."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness `ExpanderFuzzer` remains untouched; it still calls [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39m.., tempDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, triggering our hardened logic.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo harness or test code is modified—only core path‐resolution and Expander write [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls are updated. This fully addresses the Jazzer sanitizer’s “File path [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal” verdict.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: a87e9aa6b0374484[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggers a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception from Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer when expanding archive [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentries whose names lead to paths outside the intended output directory. The [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitial implementation of `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` simply called [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, then checked `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, but [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailed to catch certain traversal inputs. [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch was applied to:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Harden `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` by stripping leading separators, using [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcleaned[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, and explicitly rejecting absolute paths or those [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeginning with “..”.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Ensure parent directories exist in `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` by calling [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtargetPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` just before writing a new file.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDespite these changes, the fuzzer still reports a path traversal violation at [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:87[0m[39m`, indicating that the sanitizer continues to detect an escape [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the intended output directory.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Exception raised**:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Stack trace highlights**:  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `FilePathTraversal.check [0m[35m/[0m[39m checkPath [0m[35m/[0m[39m pathFirstArgHook` in the Jazzer [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:86[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` through multiple overloads  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `[0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Key observation**:  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The sanitizer flags the call to `[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` because [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`targetPath` resolves to a location outside the sandboxed parent directory [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/expander-tmp.../[0m[95moutput[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The simplistic `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproach did not eliminate all directory-traversal payloads embedded in archive [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry names.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **ArchiveEntry.resolveIn** [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Added `[0m[1;35mObjects.requireNonNull[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath, [0m[32m"parentPath must not be null"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stripped leading `[0m[35m/[0m[39m` or `\` characters from the entry name.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Built a relative normalized path:  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     String cleaned = [0m[1;35mname.replaceFirst[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"^[0m[32m[[0m[32m/\\\\[0m[32m][0m[32m+"[0m[39m, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Path rel = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcleaned[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mrel.isAbsolute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;35mrel.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m".."[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip detected: [0m[32mparent[0m[32m=%s, [0m[32mentry[0m[32m=%s, [0m[32mnormalized[0m[32m=%s"[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           parentPath, name, rel[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removed the old check that compared `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on the final [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved path.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Expander.expand** [0m[1;39m([0m[39min [0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before opening `[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, inserted:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
