[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:75[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m83[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:    default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:        final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:        final Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        return outputFile;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:79[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m86[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:                final Path parent = nullTarget ? null : [0m[1;35mtargetPath.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Failed to create directory "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Strengthen `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` to sanitize and validate entry names at the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegment level:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Normalize separators: replace all backslashes [0m[1;39m([0m[39m‘\’[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with forward slashes [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m‘[0m[35m/[0m[39m’[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Strip any leading slashes to prevent absolute-path bypass.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Split the cleaned name on ‘[0m[35m/[0m[39m’ and process each segment:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - URL‐decode only valid percent‐hex sequences [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., “%2e” → “.”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in a custom[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhelper [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor `URLDecoder.decode`, guarding against malformed escapes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Skip empty or “.” segments.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Reject any “..” segment outright by throwing `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdetected: entry name contains '..': "[0m[39m + name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - On the first segment only, reject Windows-drive patterns like “C:” or “C:\”[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif decoded.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Reconstruct a `Path` from the sanitized segments via `[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msegments…[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, then normalize it.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. After resolution, perform a final check:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path resolved = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39msanitized[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparentPath.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"Zip slip detected: [0m[32mparent[0m[32m=%s, [0m[32mentry[0m[32m=%s, [0m[32mresolved[0m[32m=%s"[0m[39m,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              parentPath, name, resolved[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This ensures that encoded or mixed‐separator traversal payloads cannot slip past[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma simple `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add a defense‐in‐depth check in `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` immediately after calling[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`resolveIn` and before invoking any filesystem write:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Path normalizedBase = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Path normalizedTarget = [0m[1;35mtargetPath.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mnormalizedTarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalizedBase[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Resolved path escapes target directory: "[0m[39m + [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalizedTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This double‐checks that even if future changes inadvertently weaken `resolveIn`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno write outside the sandbox will occur.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Reapply existing defensive steps:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the `[0m[1;35mObjects.requireNonNull[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` guard.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintain `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before writing.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation notes:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a private static helper in the `ArchiveEntry` interface [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor a shared[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for percent‐decoding segments, ensuring malformed encodings trigger an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception rather than silently bypass checks.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use only JDK classes [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `java.net.URLDecoder` or a custom decoder[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m — do [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot bring in external libraries.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoid modifying harness code or tests; this patch only touches the core [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntry` sanitization and `Expander` write guard.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & impact:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Optimality**: Segment‐level inspection is the industry best practice against[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“zip‐slip” attacks, catching sophisticated payloads like `%2e%2e%2f` or backslash [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariants.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Logic preservation**: Directory entries and valid file entries remain [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected; only entries that truly navigate above `parentPath` are rejected.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Defense-in-depth**: The second check in `Expander` ensures any future bypass[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `resolveIn` still cannot trigger a write outside the output directory.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Side effects**: Minimal performance overhead for decoding; legitimate entry [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames containing `%` may be percent‐decoded but will only be rejected if they form [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal segments. Existing functionality and tests pass unmodified.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Optional extension:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Apply the same hardened `resolveIn` logic to other archive formats [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTar, 7z[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby virtue of the shared `ArchiveEntry` interface, ensuring uniform protection [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macross all implementations.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
